### Additional Screens (Accessible via Settings or Home)
- **Net Worth Tracking** - Accessible from Home dashboard or Settings
- **Account Management** - Accessible from Settings â†’ Account Settings
- **Backup & Restore** - Accessible from Settings â†’ Data Management
- **Receipt Scanning** - Accessible from Add Transaction or dedicated button
- **Reports & Analytics** - Accessible from Budgets or Settings
- **Receipt Library** - Accessible from Receipt Scanning or Settings
- **Data Export** - Accessible from Settings â†’ Data Management
- **Family Budget Management** - Accessible from Settings â†’ Family Settings
- **Investment Tracking** - Accessible from Net Worth or Settings
- **Advanced Analytics** - Accessible from Reports & Analytics

---

## Screen Flow Summary

### Main Navigation Flow
1. **Home Dashboard** - Main landing screen with overview and quick actions
2. **Budgets** - Budget management and tracking
3. **Transactions** - Transaction list and management
4. **Goals** - Savings goals and progress tracking
5. **Settings** - App configuration and additional features

### Feature Access Flow

#### Net Worth Tracking
- **Primary Access**: Home Dashboard â†’ "Net Worth" quick action
- **Secondary Access**: Settings â†’ Account Settings â†’ Net Worth
- **Screens**: Net Worth Tracking, Add Asset/Liability

#### Account Management
- **Primary Access**: Settings â†’ Account Settings â†’ Bank Accounts
- **Screens**: Account Management, Add Account

#### Backup & Restore
- **Primary Access**: Settings â†’ Data Management â†’ Backup Data/Restore Data
- **Screens**: Backup & Restore, Data Export

#### Receipt Scanning
- **Primary Access**: Add Transaction â†’ "Add receipt photo" option
- **Secondary Access**: Home Dashboard â†’ "Scan Receipt" quick action
- **Screens**: Receipt Scanning, Receipt Library

#### Reports & Analytics
- **Primary Access**: Home Dashboard â†’ "View Reports" quick action
- **Secondary Access**: Budgets â†’ Reports tab
- **Screens**: Reports & Analytics, Data Export

### Screen Relationships

#### Core Features
- **Home Dashboard** â†’ Quick access to all major features
- **Budgets** â†’ Category management, budget insights
- **Transactions** â†’ Add transaction, receipt scanning
- **Goals** â†’ Goal tracking, progress visualization
- **Settings** â†’ App configuration, data management

#### Advanced Features
- **Net Worth** â†’ Asset/liability management, financial health overview
- **Account Management** â†’ Multiple account support, transfers
- **Backup & Restore** â†’ Data security, export/import
- **Receipt Scanning** â†’ OCR processing, receipt library
- **Reports & Analytics** â†’ Financial insights, data export

### Developer Implementation Notes

#### Navigation Implementation
- Use React Navigation with bottom tabs for main navigation
- Implement stack navigation for feature screens
- Use modal navigation for add/edit screens
- Implement deep linking for quick actions

#### Screen Dependencies
- **Net Worth** depends on Account Management for account data
- **Receipt Scanning** integrates with Transactions for automatic transaction creation
- **Backup & Restore** affects all data screens
- **Reports & Analytics** aggregates data from all other screens

#### Data Flow
- All screens share common data store (Redux/Context)
- Real-time updates across all screens
- Offline-first architecture with sync capabilities
- Secure data storage with encryption

#### UI/UX Considerations
- Consistent design language across all screens
- Responsive design for different screen sizes
- Accessibility features for all users
- Dark mode support throughout the app
- Loading states and error handling for all features

---

## Design Notes

### Color Scheme
- **Primary**: Blue (#3B82F6)
- **Success**: Green (#10B981)
- **Warning**: Yellow (#F59E0B)
- **Danger**: Red (#EF4444)
- **Neutral**: Gray (#6B7280)

### Typography
- **Headers**: Bold, 18-24px
- **Body**: Regular, 14-16px
- **Captions**: Light, 12px

### Spacing
- **Padding**: 16px standard
- **Margins**: 8px, 16px, 24px
- **Border Radius**: 8px for cards, 4px for inputs

### Icons
- Use consistent icon set (Feather, Lucide, or custom)
- Icon size: 20px for standard, 24px for emphasis
- Color: Match text color or use accent colors

### Accessibility
- Minimum touch target: 44px
- High contrast ratios
- Screen reader support
- VoiceOver/TalkBack compatibility
